/&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;b&gt;               &lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;page&quot; title=&quot;Page 1&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;layoutArea&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;column&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;; font-size: 12.000000pt;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;Shark diving&lt;/a&gt; has gained in popularity over the last decade or so. With the increasing number of operations that offer interactions with sharks, we have also seen a growing trend for some operators to use irresponsible and in some cases down right stupid and dangerous diving practices.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-wdQyDlRIdtc/VvwPAoy0ziI/AAAAAAAACaU/7txDx9PGg0gFzOHwrxL1ih4ZnZn5PInrQCKgB/s1600/_26A8544.JPG&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;266&quot; src=&quot;https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-wdQyDlRIdtc/VvwPAoy0ziI/AAAAAAAACaU/7txDx9PGg0gFzOHwrxL1ih4ZnZn5PInrQCKgB/s400/_26A8544.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;; font-size: 12.000000pt;&quot;&gt;So how can a diver find an operation that is using responsible and sustainable practices? How does he/she know if an operation is participating in conservation efforts, education and research?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-RsZY7EdgI0Q/U11ez6emKII/AAAAAAAAAz8/mpR45o1lkBszcYytKP1ibL9deT8SNGlIgCKgB/s1600/DSC_0158ab.jpg&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;265&quot; src=&quot;https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-RsZY7EdgI0Q/U11ez6emKII/AAAAAAAAAz8/mpR45o1lkBszcYytKP1ibL9deT8SNGlIgCKgB/s400/DSC_0158ab.jpg&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;; font-size: 12.000000pt;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;; font-size: 12.000000pt;&quot;&gt;Now there is a way to do exactly that. Rick McPherson, a marine biologist and conservationist has created a website, &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sustainablesharkdiving.com/&quot;&gt;www.sustainablesharkdiving.com&lt;/a&gt; that is rating shark diving operations on various criteria, helping divers in choosing who to go with. It is sort of like a trip advisor for the shark diving industry.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;; font-size: 12.000000pt;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;; font-size: 12.000000pt;&quot;&gt;We at &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;Shark Diver&lt;/a&gt; are proud to provide our divers with a &quot;Safe and Sane&quot; &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;shark diving&lt;/a&gt; experience and support research and conservation through our collaboration with the &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.marinecsi.org/&quot;&gt;Marine Conservation Science Institute&lt;/a&gt;. We are excited about Rick&#39;s new website and hope that anyone interested in shark diving will use it when choosing their next dive operation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;; font-size: 12.000000pt;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;; font-size: 12.000000pt;&quot;&gt;Here is the press release, announcing &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sustainablesharkdiving.com/&quot;&gt;www.sustainablesharkdiving.com&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;; font-size: 12.000000pt;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;San Francisco, CA &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;     &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-weight: 700;&quot;&gt;Sustainable Shark Dive Tourism Website Now Live: Best Practices and Trip Reviews &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;     &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;Sustainable Shark Diving (&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue; font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;www.sustainablesharkdiving.com&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;), a new website that provides tools and “Trip Advisor-like reviews of shark dive tourism operations around the world is now live. The website, previewed at the 2015 DEMA Show in Florida to overwhelming interest and support, has opened and now offers shark divers an opportunity to learn about best practices while helping to promote more sustainable environmental and safety within the industry.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;     &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;The popularity and growth of shark dive tourism over the past decade is undeniable. Divers increasingly want to see sharks and are willing to pay well to have close encounters with these charismatic species. For a critically threatened group such as sharks, this is good news. “&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;Over 100 million sharks die each year due to interactions with fisheries, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;“ reports Rick MacPherson, marine biologist, conservationist, and founder of the new online tool Sustainable Shark Diving “&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;I believe a living shark showcased for tourism over its lifetime is better than a dead shark used once for its fins and meat,&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;” says MacPherson. “&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;I created sustainablesharkdiving.com as a free, open access portal for tourists and dive operators to help underscore the value of healthy shark populations to tourism as well as highlight best practices and lessons learned from shark dive operations around the world.” &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;Dr Austin Gallagher, Postdoctoral Researcher at Carleton University and principal author of a ground-breaking 2015 global study of the shark diving industry, agrees, &quot;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;The value of shark diving tourism to local economies and cultures has emerged as one of the leading arguments for the conservation of sharks around the world.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;&quot; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;     &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;The shark dive tourism industry has already taken note of the value of this new online tool. Jorge Loria, owner of Phantom Divers, a bull shark diving operation in Playa del Carmen, Mexico, believes this tool will help create a higher standard for the growing shark diving industry, “&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;Diving with a sustainable business that is safe and educational results in a benefit to both divers and sharks because the more we know about sharks the better we can protect them.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;” Mike Neumann, owner of Beqa Adventure Divers in Fiji agrees: “&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;This will be a game changer and a huge step towards propelling the shark diving industry towards a more long term sustainable model&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;.”&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;     &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;Sustainable Shark Diving fills an industry need by providing a free, one-stop source for best safety and environmental practices and guidelines that have been established around the world for the viewing of sharks (and their flat cousins the rays). “&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;Sustainable Shark Diving offers visitors a compilation of shark diving best practices and guidelines,&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;” explains MacPherson. “&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;You can search by shark species or by region. Whether you want to dive with white sharks, whale sharks, oceanic whitetip, bull, nurse, or any species, you will find the most currently accepted sustainability guidelines for that type of experience.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;”&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;     &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;Importantly, Sustainable Shark Diving features a Trip Advisor-like review section that allows divers to rate their experience with any shark dive operation against a set of sustainability criteria that includes safety, environmental performance, staff interactions, and overall educational/conservation value. &quot;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;This tool has enormous potential to begin pushing the entire global industry closer to sustainability and accountability”&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;, says Dr Gallagher. “&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;By allowing the tourists themselves - the lifeblood of this and any tourism industry - to rank the performance, safety, and environmental ethics of operators around the world, the industry as a whole becomes more transparent and we can promote the good and hopefully phase out the bad.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;&quot;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;     &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-weight: 700;&quot;&gt;ABOUT RICK MACPHERSON, FOUNDER &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;     &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;Rick MacPherson is a marine ecologist and conservationist with three decades of experience in solving environmental challenges. He has a particular focus and interest in the intersection of conservation and marine tourism. As a PADI certified diver for over 35 years, he has witnessed the decline of coral reefs and shark populations during his lifetime. In response, MacPherson has become a passionate advocate and thought leader on the role of sustainable tourism as a lever for ocean conservation. Achievements have included development of the world’s first standards for scuba diving, snorkeling, and boating; designer of the Criteria and Indicators for Sustainable Marine Tours for the Cruise Lines International Association (CLIA), and founder of the Mesoamerican Reef Tourism Initiative--the longest-running sustainable tourism project in the Americas. With a belief and expertise in collaborative solutions, MacPherson has brokered partnerships across governments, corporations, NGOs, private sector, and local communities to arrive at pragmatic solutions to complex environmental problems. He is Founder and Principal of Pelagia Consulting, a San Francisco-based ocean science and conservation think tank, where he serves as senior advisor to international NGOs and charitable foundations. In 2013, MacPherson was awarded the Oris/Scuba Diving Magazine Sea Hero of the Year Award in recognition of his achievements in ocean conservation.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;    &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;   &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;      &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;  &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;page&quot; title=&quot;Page 2&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;   &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;layoutArea&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;    &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;column&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;     &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-weight: 700;&quot;&gt;CONTACT&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;     &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: small;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;Rick MacPherson, Founder Sustainable Shark Diving &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue; font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;rickmacpherson@me.com &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: &amp;quot;arialmt&amp;quot;;&quot;&gt;+1 (510) 295-5538 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Let&#39;s go (sustainable) &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;Shark Diving&lt;/a&gt;!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Cheers,&lt;br /&gt;Martin Graf&lt;br /&gt;CEO &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;Shark Diver&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;About Shark Diver&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.   As a global leader in commercial shark diving and conservation initiatives Shark Diver has spent the past decade engaged for sharks around the world. Our blog highlights all aspects of both of these dynamic and shifting worlds. 178px; } }&lt;/style&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;ig-b- ig-b-v-24&quot; href=&quot;https://www.instagram.com/shark_diver_llc/?ref=badge&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Instagram&quot; src=&quot;//badges.instagram.com/static/images/ig-badge-view-24.png&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;What&#39;s it like to come face to face with a &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;Great White Shark&lt;/a&gt;? That is a question I get asked time and time again. With the news media portraying sharks as blood thirsty, mindless killers, just looking to eat us, most people think I have a death wish, &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;diving with sharks&lt;/a&gt;. So I thought I should share what it is really like to come face to face with one of the most feared creatures on earth.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-WDQTtGr8298/Vg0GrO5i6CI/AAAAAAAAB28/yplyLWfopjcZ9xhhJaiVAd8mMETsGtS5A/s1600/_26A5834%2BShark%2B%2523153%2Bcopy.jpg&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;266&quot; src=&quot;https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-WDQTtGr8298/Vg0GrO5i6CI/AAAAAAAAB28/yplyLWfopjcZ9xhhJaiVAd8mMETsGtS5A/s400/_26A5834%2BShark%2B%2523153%2Bcopy.jpg&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Here is a little video that shows how most people think an encounter with a &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;shark&lt;/a&gt; will be like.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;object width=&quot;320&quot; height=&quot;266&quot; class=&quot;BLOG_video_class&quot; id=&quot;BLOG_video-917b5aaa4caa4814&quot; classid=&quot;clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000&quot; codebase=&quot;http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0&quot;&gt;&lt;param name=&quot;movie&quot; value=&quot;https://www.youtube.com/get_player&quot;&gt;&lt;param name=&quot;bgcolor&quot; value=&quot;#FFFFFF&quot;&gt;&lt;param name=&quot;allowfullscreen&quot; value=&quot;true&quot;&gt;&lt;param name=&quot;flashvars&quot; value=&quot;flvurl=https://redirector.googlevideo.com/videoplayback?id%3D917b5aaa4caa4814%26itag%3D5%26source%3Dblogger%26requiressl%3Dyes%26app%3Dblogger%26cmo%3Dsecure_transport%3Dyes%26cmo%3Dsensitive_content%3Dyes%26ip%3D0.0.0.0%26ipbits%3D0%26expire%3D1495432879%26sparams%3Dip,ipbits,expire,id,itag,source,requiressl%26signature%3D847F46424DCBDEF25ABD3A5274C6EBDF908F27C9.B7A1B21D359AD406055D01A482B97E42435773A6%26key%3Dck2&amp;amp;iurl=http://video.google.com/ThumbnailServer2?app%3Dblogger%26contentid%3D917b5aaa4caa4814%26offsetms%3D5000%26itag%3Dw160%26sigh%3D7iuFRrCB7Hd_JE0Yh1lY7uoQ5Ro&amp;amp;autoplay=0&amp;amp;ps=blogger&quot;&gt;&lt;embed src=&quot;https://www.youtube.com/get_player&quot; type=&quot;application/x-shockwave-flash&quot; width=&quot;320&quot; height=&quot;266&quot; bgcolor=&quot;#FFFFFF&quot; flashvars=&quot;flvurl=https://redirector.googlevideo.com/videoplayback?id%3D917b5aaa4caa4814%26itag%3D5%26source%3Dblogger%26requiressl%3Dyes%26app%3Dblogger%26cmo%3Dsecure_transport%3Dyes%26cmo%3Dsensitive_content%3Dyes%26ip%3D0.0.0.0%26ipbits%3D0%26expire%3D1495432879%26sparams%3Dip,ipbits,expire,id,itag,source,requiressl%26signature%3D847F46424DCBDEF25ABD3A5274C6EBDF908F27C9.B7A1B21D359AD406055D01A482B97E42435773A6%26key%3Dck2&amp;iurl=http://video.google.com/ThumbnailServer2?app%3Dblogger%26contentid%3D917b5aaa4caa4814%26offsetms%3D5000%26itag%3Dw160%26sigh%3D7iuFRrCB7Hd_JE0Yh1lY7uoQ5Ro&amp;autoplay=0&amp;ps=blogger&quot; allowFullScreen=&quot;true&quot; /&gt;&lt;/object&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The reality it is more like the &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;sharks&lt;/a&gt; swim by slowly, looking you straight into the eyes and showing absolutely no signs that they want to eat you.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-r-4zIIZfuOg/Vg0eTH4xqdI/AAAAAAAAB5s/pW9ehVKOrcksJhcOojZC3MoanPf_SyPLA/s1600/August%2B10%2Bmartin-6.JPG&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;282&quot; src=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-r-4zIIZfuOg/Vg0eTH4xqdI/AAAAAAAAB5s/pW9ehVKOrcksJhcOojZC3MoanPf_SyPLA/s400/August%2B10%2Bmartin-6.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;When I first started diving with &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;white sharks&lt;/a&gt;, what struck me is the fact that it is not scary at all. I&#39;m by no means the only one that feels that way. In 15 seasons of taking divers to meet these awesome creatures, the most common reaction when coming face to face with a &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;great white shark&lt;/a&gt; is just awe. Even divers who saw &quot;Jaws&quot; and joined us expecting a huge adrenaline rush, mostly are just blown away by the experience and don&#39;t find it the least bit scary. The scariest part of the expedition is the anticipation of that first meeting.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Mw5BoT_RGOg/UiEE9Oj_EgI/AAAAAAAAAOo/SgKe0QWz41IjksLm_wBj8cCElN3YckWkQ/s1600/%252356.jpg&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;300&quot; src=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Mw5BoT_RGOg/UiEE9Oj_EgI/AAAAAAAAAOo/SgKe0QWz41IjksLm_wBj8cCElN3YckWkQ/s400/%252356.jpg&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I remember that after about 3 trips to &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;Guadalupe Island&lt;/a&gt; I started thinking &quot;I&#39;ve seen it&quot; and didn&#39;t expect to do this for much longer. Well, at the time I didn&#39;t expect to be in the cage and have &quot;Shredder&quot; swim by to check me out. When he looked me straight into the eye, something happened. I realized that this huge shark is focused on me, that he was individually checking everyone out.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;table align=&quot;center&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; class=&quot;tr-caption-container&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style=&quot;text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IIxauZBTekA/VK2OHK4cNjI/AAAAAAAABNg/IOPcThFLmoEGosv9IoZXX88D3Pwdykbfw/s1600/Shredder.jpg&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;336&quot; src=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IIxauZBTekA/VK2OHK4cNjI/AAAAAAAABNg/IOPcThFLmoEGosv9IoZXX88D3Pwdykbfw/s400/Shredder.jpg&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class=&quot;tr-caption&quot; style=&quot;text-align: center;&quot;&gt;Shredder&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Thinking back, that is when I fell in love with those &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;sharks&lt;/a&gt;. Now as I always say to our divers. I love those sharks, but it is not a mutual feeling. That is perfectly OK. I love them for what they are, awesome predators, not mindless killers, but certainly no harmless pets either.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-wdQyDlRIdtc/VvwPAoy0ziI/AAAAAAAACaQ/hboRihRXLMAY082im3b1aWTu3a03tnpbA/s1600/_26A8544.JPG&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;266&quot; src=&quot;https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-wdQyDlRIdtc/VvwPAoy0ziI/AAAAAAAACaQ/hboRihRXLMAY082im3b1aWTu3a03tnpbA/s400/_26A8544.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I don&#39;t feel the need to tell everyone that these &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;sharks&lt;/a&gt; love me and that I can go hold onto their fins, because they accept me as one of their own. Come to think of it, I&#39;m glad that they don&#39;t treat me as one of their own. Even though I&#39;m not a small person, in terms of &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;white shark&lt;/a&gt; size, I would be a very, very small shark. &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;White sharks&lt;/a&gt; definitely are into having their personal space and don&#39;t react kindly to a smaller individual invading that space. I&#39;ve seen what they do to a smaller shark that is doing this.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-V4T3pkuqM4k/U_kNDFmFtwI/AAAAAAAABEE/qTLNEBRSXsYMw_2tROHoGyCt9bNTtj6bA/s1600/1-68.JPG&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;243&quot; src=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-V4T3pkuqM4k/U_kNDFmFtwI/AAAAAAAABEE/qTLNEBRSXsYMw_2tROHoGyCt9bNTtj6bA/s400/1-68.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I&#39;ve been diving with sharks for over 15 years and I&#39;m excited every time I&#39;m about to get into the water with them. I find them fascinating and discovered that they are generally very cautious and even shy, not the mindless killers the media makes them out to be at all. Last season I saw 3 &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;white sharks&lt;/a&gt; that got scared by a towel that fell overboard and drifted down. 2 of them checked it out and got the heck out of there. One of them kept circling it, approaching it and jerking away, when the towel moved a little. He kept doing that until both he and the towel went out of sight.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I hope that I have given you an idea of what it feels like to come face to face with a &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;great white shark&lt;/a&gt;. If you really want to know, there is no substitute for experiencing it for yourself and I hope you&#39;ll get that chance. It is an experience you&#39;ll never forget. When you do go out, remember that while we don&#39;t have to fear these sharks, we definitely have to respect them.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-iu9rl1x2JAk/Va_SyzqlG6I/AAAAAAAABnI/HRhQ56wqfcQyejdXr6BEgAnJ5YL9NHXEQ/s1600/close%2Bup%2Bwith%2Bcamera%2Bblog%2Bres.jpg&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;273&quot; src=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-iu9rl1x2JAk/Va_SyzqlG6I/AAAAAAAABnI/HRhQ56wqfcQyejdXr6BEgAnJ5YL9NHXEQ/s400/close%2Bup%2Bwith%2Bcamera%2Bblog%2Bres.jpg&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;We at &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;Shark Diver&lt;/a&gt; promote &quot;Safe and Sane Shark Diving&quot; that respects the sharks and the environment. We hope to see you on one of our expeditions to Guadalupe Island.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Let&#39;s go shark diving!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Cheers,&lt;br /&gt;Martin Graf&lt;br /&gt;CEO &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;Shark Diver &lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;About Shark Diver&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.   As a global leader in commercial shark diving and conservation initiatives Shark Diver has spent the past decade engaged for sharks around the world. scheme="http://www.blogger.com/atom/ns#" term="aggressive shark"/><category scheme="http://www.blogger.com/atom/ns#" term="bull shark"/><category scheme="http://www.blogger.com/atom/ns#" term="cage diving"/><category scheme="http://www.blogger.com/atom/ns#" term="great white shark"/><category scheme="http://www.blogger.com/atom/ns#" term="guadalupe island"/><category scheme="http://www.blogger.com/atom/ns#" term="shark attack"/><category scheme="http://www.blogger.com/atom/ns#" term="shark media"/><category scheme="http://www.blogger.com/atom/ns#" term="tiger shark"/><title type='text'>Who is more aggressive,  a Bull Shark or  a Great White?</title><content type='html'>&lt;script&gt;  window.fbAsyncInit = function() {     FB.init({       appId      : &#39;1049102595151768&#39;,       xfbml      : true,       version    : &#39;v2.5&#39;     });   };    (function(d, s, id){      var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];      if (d.getElementById(id)) {return;}      js = d.createElement(s); js.id = id;      js.src = &quot;//connect.facebook.net/en_US/sdk.js&quot;;      fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);    }(document, &#39;script&#39;, &#39;facebook-jssdk&#39;)); &lt;/script&gt; &lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;fb-like&quot; data-share=&quot;true&quot; data-show-faces=&quot;true&quot; data-width=&quot;450&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;style&gt;.ig-b- { display: inline-block; } .ig-b- img { visibility: hidden; } .ig-b-:hover { background-position: 0 -60px; } .ig-b-:active { background-position: 0 -120px; } .ig-b-v-24 { width: 137px; height: 24px; background: url(//badges.instagram.com/static/images/ig-badge-view-sprite-24.png) no-repeat 0 0; } @media only screen and (-webkit-min-device-pixel-ratio: 2), only screen and (min--moz-device-pixel-ratio: 2), only screen and (-o-min-device-pixel-ratio: 2 / 1), only screen and (min-device-pixel-ratio: 2), only screen and (min-resolution: 192dpi), only screen and (min-resolution: 2dppx) { .ig-b-v-24 { background-image: url(//badges.instagram.com/static/images/ig-badge-view-sprite-24@2x.png); background-size: 160px 178px; } }&lt;/style&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;ig-b- ig-b-v-24&quot; href=&quot;https://www.instagram.com/shark_diver_llc/?ref=badge&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Instagram&quot; src=&quot;//badges.instagram.com/static/images/ig-badge-view-24.png&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;We hear a lot about how aggressive shark are. Some people think that if they encounter a &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;shark&lt;/a&gt; in the ocean, they will get bit. This kind of thinking is at least partially fueled by the media that seems to portray any encounter with a shark as a near death experience.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I&#39;ve been diving with &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/dive-packages/great-white-shark-diving/&quot;&gt;Great White&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/dive-packages/bull-shark-diving-fiji/&quot;&gt;Bull&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/dive-packages/tiger-shark-diving/&quot;&gt;Tiger Sharks&lt;/a&gt; for over 15 years now and have found that most sharks are actually pretty shy and not very aggressive. Despite the fact that &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;shark&lt;/a&gt; bites and attacks are extremely rare, the common perception is that they are dangerous. When it comes to what species is most dangerous, people tell me that because they have more testosterone than any other shark, Bull Sharks are the most aggressive and therefore the most dangerous to humans.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;It is true, that since &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/dive-packages/bull-shark-diving-fiji/&quot;&gt;Bull Sharks&lt;/a&gt; can swim and hunt in very shallow, brackish and even fresh water, they tend to be in much closer proximity to humans than Tiger or Great White Sharks. This obviously leads to a greater chance of an encounter with them, which can result in an occasional bite or attack. Such bites however remain extremely rare. Last year there were 96 shark bites with 6 fatalities reported worldwide. These numbers include all species of shark.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I think that a lot of people confuse feeding with aggression. Biting that is related to hunting or feeding has nothing to do with the testosterone level, but is simply and indication that the shark is hungry. Aggression has to do with defending their territory, establishing dominance and is usually directed toward another shark or a perceived competitor. So if we look at it that way, who is more aggressive, the &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/dive-packages/bull-shark-diving-fiji/&quot;&gt;Bull Shark&lt;/a&gt;, or the &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/dive-packages/great-white-shark-diving/&quot;&gt;Great White Shark&lt;/a&gt;?&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Well, let me show you a couple of pictures.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://2.bp.blogspot.com/--6RoX8Z7cWE/U_FfFSuYjyI/AAAAAAAABCo/hqIs8ydDyOw/s1600/Chugey.JPG&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;275&quot; src=&quot;https://2.bp.blogspot.com/--6RoX8Z7cWE/U_FfFSuYjyI/AAAAAAAABCo/hqIs8ydDyOw/s400/Chugey.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-m4Yaj2toyds/VA3MdBJbAuI/AAAAAAAABFI/BmO6511IVV0/s1600/P9120555.JPG&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;300&quot; src=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-m4Yaj2toyds/VA3MdBJbAuI/AAAAAAAABFI/BmO6511IVV0/s400/P9120555.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-V4T3pkuqM4k/U_kNDFmFtwI/AAAAAAAABEE/qTLNEBRSXsY/s1600/1-68.JPG&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;243&quot; src=&quot;https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-V4T3pkuqM4k/U_kNDFmFtwI/AAAAAAAABEE/qTLNEBRSXsY/s400/1-68.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-9WwfkWgjaW8/VUT2u0ZpXFI/AAAAAAAABZM/c1ISM723Etc/s1600/Bruce%2Bwith%2Bbite.jpg&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;285&quot; src=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-9WwfkWgjaW8/VUT2u0ZpXFI/AAAAAAAABZM/c1ISM723Etc/s400/Bruce%2Bwith%2Bbite.jpg&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;These pictures all show Great White Sharks with bite marks from their own kind. It is rare to see an adult &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/dive-packages/great-white-shark-diving/&quot;&gt;Great White Shark&lt;/a&gt; that doesn&#39;t have some kind of scar or fresh bite mark on them. These sharks are very much into keeping their &quot;personal space&quot; and it is rare for them to touch each other, without there being some biting involved. Typically when 2 &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/dive-packages/great-white-shark-diving/&quot;&gt;White Sharks&lt;/a&gt; encounter each other, they pass each other head on, to establish who is bigger. If that doesn&#39;t settle it, they tend to come back together and swim parallel with each other, to get a closer look. Now if that still doesn&#39;t settle it, the more dominant sharks usually shows the other who&#39;s boss by biting it on the head or in the gill area.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Now I want to stress that the aggression I have observed on White Sharks is shown towards other shark and not humans, or other animals in the ocean. Just like any other &quot;dangerous&quot; shark, they are not very likely to attack a human. &lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-QEiXAP98Ic0/U35OP3ga7TI/AAAAAAAAA48/-CpUN98Y2-s/s1600/XD5V0095.jpg&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;242&quot; src=&quot;https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-QEiXAP98Ic0/U35OP3ga7TI/AAAAAAAAA48/-CpUN98Y2-s/s400/XD5V0095.jpg&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jlG8YSanWKE/U35NLo1fPsI/AAAAAAAAA5M/GK_PtPMYMk0/s1600/XD5V1869-293.JPG&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;266&quot; src=&quot;https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jlG8YSanWKE/U35NLo1fPsI/AAAAAAAAA5M/GK_PtPMYMk0/s400/XD5V1869-293.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;table align=&quot;center&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; class=&quot;tr-caption-container&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style=&quot;text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-0C6s5vmYSBs/Vs33rhcdi3I/AAAAAAAACRY/BtOgnWrYCKw/s1600/_26A0886.JPG&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;266&quot; src=&quot;https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-0C6s5vmYSBs/Vs33rhcdi3I/AAAAAAAACRY/BtOgnWrYCKw/s400/_26A0886.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class=&quot;tr-caption&quot; style=&quot;text-align: center;&quot;&gt;Add caption&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;&lt;table align=&quot;center&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; class=&quot;tr-caption-container&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style=&quot;text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mlKiW8mT9vs/Vs4BnkfzanI/AAAAAAAACRs/kgttOYjLNgE/s1600/_26A5402.JPG&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;266&quot; src=&quot;https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mlKiW8mT9vs/Vs4BnkfzanI/AAAAAAAACRs/kgttOYjLNgE/s400/_26A5402.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class=&quot;tr-caption&quot; style=&quot;text-align: center;&quot;&gt;2 of these sharks just got a tuna head, they show no aggression.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td class=&quot;tr-caption&quot; style=&quot;text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;&lt;br /&gt;In the pictures above, you can see lot&#39;s of &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/dive-packages/bull-shark-diving-fiji/&quot;&gt;Bull Sharks&lt;/a&gt; swimming very close together and there doesn&#39;t seem to be any aggression. I&#39;ve seen over 70 of those sharks, without noticing any that had bite marks on them. This is something that definitely can&#39;t be said about &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/dive-packages/great-white-shark-diving/&quot;&gt;Great Whites&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;It never ceases to amaze me, how little we know about sharks and how much of what we &quot;know&quot; is actually wrong. We tend to think that something like testosterone will have the same effect in sharks as it does in humans. On the flip side of the &quot;sharks are mindless killer&quot; attitude, there is the &quot;sharks want to be hugged&quot; crowd, that is trying to show how harmless these sharks are by riding, grabbing, flipping and hugging them.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Let&#39;s appreciate the sharks for who and what they are. They are not mindless killers, but neither are they harmless pets. As I always say, &quot;I absolutely love &quot;my&quot; sharks, but it is not a mutual feeling and that is perfectly fine with me&quot;. I don&#39;t feel the need to assign human emotions to them, I love em just they way they are.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Cheers,&lt;br /&gt;Martin Graf&lt;br /&gt;CEO Shark Diver&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;About Shark Diver&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.   As a global leader in commercial shark diving and conservation initiatives Shark Diver has spent the past decade engaged for sharks around the world. Our blog highlights all aspects of both of these dynamic and shifting worlds. /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;It looks like our friends in Fiji made it through Cyclone Winston, the worst in history.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Here is &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.blogger.com/profile/06787762757245289307&quot;&gt;Mike&#39;s&lt;/a&gt; first hand report. &lt;a href=&quot;http://fijisharkdiving.blogspot.com/2016/02/back-in-business.html?spref=fb&quot;&gt;http://fijisharkdiving.blogspot.com/2016/02/back-in-business.html?spref=fb&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;table align=&quot;center&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; class=&quot;tr-caption-container&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style=&quot;text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-kn22sT79rTg/VsrB5EnmgAI/AAAAAAAAO1s/SzZa_EAQrok/s1600/12771700_1106869759345958_6960671292674072_o.jpg&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;266&quot; src=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-kn22sT79rTg/VsrB5EnmgAI/AAAAAAAAO1s/SzZa_EAQrok/s400/12771700_1106869759345958_6960671292674072_o.jpg&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class=&quot;tr-caption&quot; style=&quot;text-align: center;&quot;&gt;A picture of the devastation.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;i&gt;Back in Business!&lt;/i&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;We&#39;re opening tomorrow.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;But first.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;This has been &lt;a href=&quot;http://mashable.com/2016/02/20/tropical-cyclone-winston-strongest/#MaBbgmyPf5qs&quot;&gt;the worst cyclone to ever hit the SoPac&lt;/a&gt;, and one of the very worst globally. &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;Our thoughts go to the families of the deceased and missing, to the many  who got injured, to the countless displaced, many of whom have &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.facebook.com/media/set/?set=a.1106865142679753.1073743765.207532522613024&amp;amp;type=3&quot;&gt;literally lost &lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://www.facebook.com/media/set/?set=a.1106865142679753.1073743765.207532522613024&amp;amp;type=3&quot;&gt;everything&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;But this is Fiji.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;Yes the widespread stoicism in the face of the onrushing onslaught may  have seemed peculiar - but the flip side is that after the event, there  is no drama whatsoever as instead of lamenting and waiting for others to  help, we get up, dust ourselves off and carry on.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;Case in point, the power and water are miraculously back on, and everybody is &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.facebook.com/media/set/?set=a.1107368805962720.1073743767.207532522613024&amp;amp;type=3&quot;&gt;busy cleaning up and helping friends and neighbors to get back on their feet&lt;/a&gt;.  And a big bravo to Government who has been handling this admirably  right from the get go, and who continues show leadership by being  proactive, efficient and effective all throughout the country.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;I also want to thank our friends.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;Your outpouring of support has been frankly humbling, and we all thank  you for that. No we really don&#39;t need anything - but should you want to  make a valuable contribution, please make a donation to the &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.fijitimes.com/story.aspx?id=342687&quot;&gt;Fiji Red Cross&lt;/a&gt; or to the &lt;a href=&quot;http://fijivillage.com/news/NDMO-on-standby-as-TC-Winston-approaches-Fiji--r92k5s/&quot;&gt;Prime Minister&#39;s Disaster Relief and Rehabilitation Fund&lt;/a&gt; as right now, those are by far the most effective venues for quickly getting the right help to the affected people.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;Thank you very much.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-QEiXAP98Ic0/U35OP3ga7TI/AAAAAAAAA48/-CpUN98Y2-s/s1600/XD5V0095.jpg&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;242&quot; src=&quot;https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-QEiXAP98Ic0/U35OP3ga7TI/AAAAAAAAA48/-CpUN98Y2-s/s400/XD5V0095.jpg&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;Anyway, we&#39;re open for business.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;Can&#39;t wait to have my first look at Shark Reef that has been battered by  phenomenal seas. We&#39;ve recently established a shallow nursery for  different endangered Giant Clams, and I&#39;m fearing the worst - but who  knows, we here are resilient.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;Keep watching this space!&amp;nbsp;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://fijisharkdiving.blogspot.com/2016/02/back-in-business.html?spref=fb&quot;&gt;http://fijisharkdiving.blogspot.com/2016/02/back-in-business.html?spref=fb&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;We are all glad you made it through OK and are looking forward to &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/dive-packages/bull-shark-diving-fiji/&quot;&gt;diving with you in May&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;Cheers!&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;Martin Graf&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: justify;&quot;&gt;CEO &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;Shark Diver&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;About Shark Diver&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.   As a global leader in commercial shark diving and conservation initiatives Shark Diver has spent the past decade engaged for sharks around the world. Our blog highlights all aspects of both of these dynamic and shifting worlds.  window.fbAsyncInit = function() {     FB.init({       appId      : &#39;1049102595151768&#39;,       xfbml      : true,       version    : &#39;v2.5&#39;     });   };    (function(d, s, id){      var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0]; } @media only screen and (-webkit-min-device-pixel-ratio: 2), only screen and (min--moz-device-pixel-ratio: 2), only screen and (-o-min-device-pixel-ratio: 2 / 1), only screen and (min-device-pixel-ratio: 2), only screen and (min-resolution: 192dpi), only screen and (min-resolution: 2dppx) { .ig-b-v-24 { background-image: url(//badges.instagram.com/static/images/ig-badge-view-sprite-24@2x.png); /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;We in the shark conservation field have been saying for years that a &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;shark&lt;/a&gt; is worth more alive than dead. We have been citing various examples of how a live shark can bring a lot more money to an area through tourism than it would being sold one time for it&#39;s meat or fins.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/--0w6g4Xr0Ko/VsIzj4qPDBI/AAAAAAAACPg/Prow0II0fYs/s1600/_26A5839%2BShark%2B%2523153copyright.jpg&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;261&quot; src=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/--0w6g4Xr0Ko/VsIzj4qPDBI/AAAAAAAACPg/Prow0II0fYs/s400/_26A5839%2BShark%2B%2523153copyright.jpg&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;There are a lot of conservationists who are advocating activities like shark diving to accomplish that goal, while others are pointing to the problems those operations can create. The problem is, how do we know if the outfit we plan on going with is taking conservation serious? How do we know who to go with?&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;table align=&quot;center&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; class=&quot;tr-caption-container&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style=&quot;text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-rtcB0mQmLPs/VeojtHxfM7I/AAAAAAAABwc/fw1fpUhRxM4/s1600/GOPR0708.JPG&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;220&quot; src=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-rtcB0mQmLPs/VeojtHxfM7I/AAAAAAAABwc/fw1fpUhRxM4/s400/GOPR0708.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class=&quot;tr-caption&quot; style=&quot;text-align: center;&quot;&gt;Diving safely, inside a cage at Guadalupe Island&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;Well, now there is a way, or to be more precise, there will be a way. &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.rickmacpherson.com/about&quot;&gt;Rick McPherson&lt;/a&gt;, a well respected conservationist is creating a website &lt;a href=&quot;http://sustainablesharkdiving.com/&quot;&gt;sustainablesharkdiving.com&lt;/a&gt; that is going to be sort of&amp;nbsp; a trip advisor for shark diving.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This is how Rick describes it himself&lt;b&gt;&lt;i&gt; &quot;&lt;a href=&quot;http://sustainablesharkdiving.com/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;SustainableSharkDiving.com&lt;/a&gt; &amp;nbsp;was created as a free, online tool for the rapidly growing shark dive  tourism community to make more informed choices about the businesses  shark divers choose to support, recognize those businesses employing  sustainable best practices, and encourage businesses that may need to  improve their environmental performance to ensure the safety of both  their clients and sharks. This is an experiment to see if consumer  voices can help build a stronger, safer, more sustainable industry.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This website will give the customers the ability to rate the dive operations, not just on their service, but also on their practices. Categories for the ratings include: are they following good practices in their interactions with the &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;sharks&lt;/a&gt;, are they educating their customers, are they supporting the local community etc.?&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Rick still need some funds to complete the website. He has a gofund me page, where you can support his efforts. Please send him a few dollars. He is not asking for much and the website can really make a difference and be a valuable tool for those divers interested in supporting sustainable shark diving.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;i&gt; &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Please click on the following link to make a donation: &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.gofundme.com/sharkdiving&quot;&gt;https://www.gofundme.com/sharkdiving&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Let&#39;s go &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;shark diving&lt;/a&gt;!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Cheers,&lt;br /&gt;Martin Graf&lt;br /&gt;CEO Shark Diver&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;About Shark Diver&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;fb-like&quot; data-share=&quot;true&quot; data-show-faces=&quot;true&quot; data-width=&quot;450&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;style&gt;.ig-b- { display: inline-block; } .ig-b- img { visibility: hidden; } .ig-b-:hover { background-position: 0 -60px; } .ig-b-:active { background-position: 0 -120px; } .ig-b-v-24 { width: 137px; height: 24px; background: only screen and (-o-min-device-pixel-ratio: 2 / 1), only screen and (min-device-pixel-ratio: 2), only screen and (min-resolution: 192dpi), only screen and (min-resolution: 2dppx) { .ig-b-v-24 { background-image: url(//badges.instagram.com/static/images/ig-badge-view-sprite-24@2x.png); background-size: 160px 178px; } }&lt;/style&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;ig-b- ig-b-v-24&quot; href=&quot;https://www.instagram.com/shark_diver_llc/?ref=badge&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Instagram&quot; src=&quot;//badges.instagram.com/static/images/ig-badge-view-24.png&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Every time a deadly shark attack occurs, people start pointing out what kills more people than sharks each year. This led me to think of a different question. What kills fewer people than sharks each year? Do you know anything that kills people, but fewer than 6 people worldwide? There might be something, but I haven&#39;t found it yet. So keep that question in mind, when you read the following.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-BFcoaiu_8ys/Vc5CrD66SbI/AAAAAAAABq0/ShpJvPpg9vc/s1600/_26A1153.JPG&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;266&quot; src=&quot;https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-BFcoaiu_8ys/Vc5CrD66SbI/AAAAAAAABq0/ShpJvPpg9vc/s400/_26A1153.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;A record number of global shark attacks is making the news these days. As expected, the headlines proclaiming this fact vary, along with the tone of the article accompanying them.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://news.discovery.com/&quot;&gt;Discovery.com&lt;/a&gt; has a headline that says: &lt;a href=&quot;http://news.discovery.com/animals/sharks/record-number-of-shark-attacks-in-2015-160208.htm&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&quot;Record number of shark attacks in 2015&quot;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt; and their article goes on to mention all the places those attacks have happened and how those numbers increased. &lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;Shark attacks hit an all time high last year, with the United States  leading all nations in numbers of such attacks, according to the  University of Florida&#39;s &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.flmnh.ufl.edu/fish/isaf/home&quot;&gt;International Shark Attack File&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;Climate change, recovering shark populations and more people in the  water help to explain the high number of recorded shark attacks for  2015: 98, including six fatalities. All of the attacks were unprovoked.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-H6O4EhyrKA0/Vg0erLpeCkI/AAAAAAAAB60/Tu-TQQ5rVzk/s1600/_26A6208.jpg&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;255&quot; src=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-H6O4EhyrKA0/Vg0erLpeCkI/AAAAAAAAB60/Tu-TQQ5rVzk/s400/_26A6208.jpg&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Discovery stresses the fact that all of those attacks were unprovoked and is careful to point out that we can expect an increase in those numbers. They stress the fact that the number of fatal attacks doubled in 2015 versus 2014.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&quot;Sharks plus humans equals attacks,&quot; George Burgess, curator of  the file, which houses the globe&#39;s clearinghouse of shark attack data,  said in a press release. &quot;As our population continues to rapidly grow  and shark populations slowly recover, we’re going to see more  interactions.&quot;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;2015 broke the prior record, which was set in 2000. That year, there  were 88 attacks. 2015 further saw double the number of deaths from shark  attacks versus 2014.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;table align=&quot;center&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; class=&quot;tr-caption-container&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style=&quot;text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-jCm23NlS9_I/VW5K6fsZo9I/AAAAAAAABb0/OdEYGTLQChw/s1600/_26A6811.JPG&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;266&quot; src=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-jCm23NlS9_I/VW5K6fsZo9I/AAAAAAAABb0/OdEYGTLQChw/s400/_26A6811.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td class=&quot;tr-caption&quot; style=&quot;text-align: center;&quot;&gt;Bull Sharks swimming along divers in Fiji&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;Yes, the number of fatalities doubled versus 2014, but what they fail to mention is that the 2014 number was unusually low and only about half the annual average.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;From the &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.flmnh.ufl.edu/fish/isaf/worldwide-summary&quot;&gt;International Shark Attack File&lt;/a&gt; summary: &lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: purple;&quot;&gt;Significantly, worldwide there were only six fatalities (producing a  6.1% fatality rate) resulting from unprovoked attacks (two in Reunion  and single incidents in Australia, New Caledonia, Hawaii, and Egypt).  &amp;nbsp;The six attacks matched the annual average of the previous decade.&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: purple;&quot;&gt;This total is remarkably low given the billions of human-hours spent in  the water each year.  &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: purple;&quot;&gt;      &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: purple;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: black;&quot;&gt;Discovery is also giving some good advice on how to avoid a shark attack, but not without prefacing it with &lt;i&gt;&quot;To avoid adding to the yearly tally&quot;&lt;/i&gt;, implying that not following that advice would lead to a shark attack. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: purple;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: black;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;To avoid adding to the yearly tally, Burgess and his team advise not to  swim at dusk, dawn or night. They also say not to wear shiny jewelry in  the water, and not to swim where people are fishing, where fish are  schooling or where seabirds are feeding.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: purple;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: black;&quot;&gt;It&#39;s not until the very end of their article that they mention that there is really no reason to worry by saying this. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;Even with 2015&#39;s record-breaking number of shark attacks, your chances  of experiencing such a risky encounter are very slim. Burgess reminded  that the following culprits killed more people than sharks last year:  spiders, dogs and lightning.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: black;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: black;&quot;&gt;So Discovery&#39;s headline could just as easily have said &quot;Spiders, dogs and lightning kill more people than sharks!&quot; but then again, who would read such an article? I&#39;m really disappointed that an outlet that is supposedly meant to educate on nature and science, is stooping to sensationalizing and spreading fear instead.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: black;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-z-Tow5PnIfA/Vg0ezueajkI/AAAAAAAAB7E/znk8JzDK2UM/s1600/_26A6367.jpg&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;267&quot; src=&quot;https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-z-Tow5PnIfA/Vg0ezueajkI/AAAAAAAAB7E/znk8JzDK2UM/s400/_26A6367.jpg&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: black;&quot;&gt;On the other hand, an outlet not usually known for holding back on sensational headlines, &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.fox13news.com/&quot;&gt;FOX 13 news&lt;/a&gt; in Tampa Bay had this headline: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://www.fox13news.com/news/local-news/86680742-story&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: #674ea7;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight: normal;&quot;&gt;Researchers: 2015 breaks shark attack record, but don&#39;t panic.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: blue;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: black;&quot;&gt;They start their article by saying: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: #351c75;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;A record number of unprovoked shark attacks in 2015 prompted University of Florida researchers to find out why.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: #351c75;&quot;&gt;&lt;i&gt;The school released its report on what might be behind the 98 attacks - a number which breaks the 2000 record of 88 attacks. &lt;/i&gt;&lt;i&gt;However, researchers said the increase should not be cause of alarm.  Although there were more attacks in 2015, fatality rate was half that of  2000. Also, the increase in attacks was likely due to a growing human  population, not a growing hunger amongst sharks for human flesh.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;b&gt; &lt;/b&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Kudos to FOX 13 in Tampa Bay for reporting a shark attack story factually, without any sensationalism! Who knew that the mainstream media could do a better job at covering this story than a science network?&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Cheers,&lt;br /&gt;Martin Graf&lt;br /&gt;CEO &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;Shark Diver&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;About Shark Diver&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.   As a global leader in commercial shark diving and conservation initiatives Shark Diver has spent the past decade engaged for sharks around the world. Our blog highlights all aspects of both of these dynamic and shifting worlds. /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;h1 class=&quot;title&quot;&gt;Bull Shark Diving Fiji&lt;/h1&gt;Bull Sharks in Fiji are calling you in May of 2016.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Experience  what many call the world&#39;s best shark dive. We are diving with big, really big &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/dive-packages/bull-shark-diving-fiji/&quot;&gt;bull sharks&lt;/a&gt;. The sharks at the Shark Reef Marine Reserve are up to 12 ft. long.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-jlG8YSanWKE/U35NLo1fPsI/AAAAAAAAA5M/GK_PtPMYMk0/s1600/XD5V1869-293.JPG&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;265&quot; src=&quot;https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-jlG8YSanWKE/U35NLo1fPsI/AAAAAAAAA5M/GK_PtPMYMk0/s400/XD5V1869-293.JPG&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://fijisharkdive.com/&quot;&gt;Beqa Adventure Divers&lt;/a&gt; will  take us out to shark reef, where we will be diving with as many as 70  bull sharks at a time, with the occasional tiger shark showing up for a  visit. If that is not enough, during our safety stop we will be  surrounded by scores of black- and white-tip reef-sharks, making for the  perfect end to an unforgettable dive. On our non &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;shark diving&lt;/a&gt; days,  we&#39;ll go out and explore the soft corals and wrecks of Beqa Lagoon.  Discover what over a decade of conservation efforts have resulted in!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;iframe allowfullscreen=&quot;allowfullscreen&quot; frameborder=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;281&quot; src=&quot;//player.vimeo.com/video/110873549&quot; width=&quot;500&quot;&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This May, &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/dive-packages/bull-shark-diving-fiji/&quot;&gt;Shark Diver&lt;/a&gt;&#39;s CEO Martin Graf is personally going to lead you on this shark lover&#39;s dream vacation! &lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;We will be staying at the luxurious &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.thepearlsouthpacific.com/&quot;&gt;Pearl South Pacific Resort&lt;/a&gt; in Pacific  Harbor,&amp;nbsp; where we&#39;ll feast on a delicious breakfast buffet each day, to  prepare us for the exciting shark diving that lies ahead.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span id=&quot;goog_39251575&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://www.blogger.com/&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span id=&quot;goog_39251576&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;How could our loving sharks possibly hurt them? After all, we want to protect them and are fighting those who are hurting them. Why would I even suggest such a ridiculous thing?&lt;span style=&quot;color: white;&quot;&gt;shark diving, cage diving, swimming with sharks, Guadalupe Island, Great White Shark, shark conservation&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;OK, lets look at what is going on. I have written about &lt;i&gt;what&lt;/i&gt; various conservation&amp;nbsp; groups are doing &lt;a href=&quot;http://sharkdivers.blogspot.com/2014/02/how-can-you-safe-sharks.html&quot;&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;. This time I want to focus on &lt;i&gt;how&lt;/i&gt; they are doing it.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Most of us are interested in shark conservation because we love &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.sharkdiver.com/&quot;&gt;sharks&lt;/a&gt;. This love is a powerful motivator to get us to act and and actually do something, instead of just standing on the sidelines. That same love for the sharks is also what can make our efforts ineffective. We tend to argue from the heart and demonize the ones that don&#39;t agree with us.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://scontent-lax3-1.xx.fbcdn.net/hphotos-xfa1/v/t1.0-9/1972274_606213262798867_1594012106_n.jpg?oh=2bc1d7bac4c8c5b17fda995cb75ff97b&amp;amp;oe=57316F30&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; height=&quot;225&quot; src=&quot;https://scontent-lax3-1.xx.fbcdn.net/hphotos-xfa1/v/t1.0-9/1972274_606213262798867_1594012106_n.jpg?oh=2bc1d7bac4c8c5b17fda995cb75ff97b&amp;amp;oe=57316F30&quot; width=&quot;400&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;Take &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.facebook.com/GoEcoPhuket/photos/pcb.606214019465458/606213262798867/?type=3&amp;amp;theater&quot;&gt;this&lt;/a&gt; post on Eco Phuket&#39;s facebook page. It shows a spearfisherman who shot a shark, cleaning his catch.
